Types

This page describes types used in the API.

AccountRole​

  • Permission levels
ValueDescription
MASTERMaster
STANDARDOperation management
READ_ONLYOperation retrieval
PERFORMANCE_MANAGEMENTReporting

  • Age range
ValueDescription

{"from":35, "to":39}35 to 39 years

{"from":45, "to":49}45 to 49 years

{"from":55, "to":59}55 to 59 years
{"from":60, "to":200}60 years or older

  • Bid strategies
ValueDescription
MAX_CLICKMaximize clicks
MAX_CONVMaximize conversions
NONEManual bidding

  • Budget control
ValueDescription

COST_CAPMaximum cost limit
NO_CAPNo bid limit
